	#Challenge to SOFA 日米地位協定への挑戦
	shared_focus = {
		id = JAP_harmonisation_initiative
		icon = dangerous_laws
		x = 64	y = 3	cost = 10
		
		cancelable = no
		
		prerequisite = {
			focus = JAP_reclaim_futenma
			focus = JAP_not_henoko
			focus = JAP_henoko_new_base 
		}
		
		available = {
		#	always = no
			ROOT = {
				any_core_state = { is_fully_controlled_by = THIS }
			}
			USA = {
				any_core_state = { is_fully_controlled_by = THIS }
			}
		}
		
		select_effect = {
			country_event = mdmosjap_japan.1640301
		}
